<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утопить.html>утопи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">utopítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утопиться.html>утопи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">utopítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топиться.html>топи́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ута́пливаться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drown oneself
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топиться.html>топи́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">topítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be melted <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of milk, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ута́пливаться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">utáplivatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утопить.html>утопи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">utopítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***уточнить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уточнить.html>уточни́ть</a> (3871)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уточнить.html>уточни́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">utočnítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уточнять.html>уточня́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to specify, to make more exact/precise</li>
<li>to inquire, to clarify by inquiring, to straighten out</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уточнять.html>уточня́ть</a> (8992)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уточнить.html>уточни́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">utočnítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уточнять.html>уточня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">utočnjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уточнить.html>уточни́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to specify, to make more exact/precise</li>
<li>to inquire, to clarify by inquiring</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утрата.html>утра́та</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">utráta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утрата.html>утра́ты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утрата.html>утра́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утрата.html>утра́т</a></b>)

***утрачивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:утрачивать.html>утра́чивать</a> (16937)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утратить.html>утра́тить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">utrátitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утрачивать.html>утра́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">utráčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утратить.html>утра́тить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lose, to forfeit</li></ol>

***утренник.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:утренник.html>у́тренник</a> (31564)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у́трен(ний)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">útren(nij)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утренник.html>у́тренник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">útrennik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утренник.html>у́тренника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утренник.html>у́тренники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утренник.html>у́тренников</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>matinee</li>
<li>predawn frost</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>у́тро</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">útro</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утренний.html>у́тренний</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">útrennij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***утро.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>у́тро</a> (232)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*(j)utro</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">morning, dawn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>у́тро</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">útro</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>у́тра</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>утра́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>у́тра</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>у́тр</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>morning
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>у́тром</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">útrom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in the morning</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>утра́м</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po <b>utrám</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">mornings</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>утру́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">k utrú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">by morning</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>утра́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">do utrá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">till morning</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>утра́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s utrá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">from morning</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>утра́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ot utrá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">from morning</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>утра́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>утра́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ot utrá do utrá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">from morning to morning</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>де́сять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часо́в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>утра́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">désjatʹ časóv utrá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">10:00 a.m.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Normally the stress falls on the first syllable, but in many set phrases with prepositions, the stress is shifted to the case ending.</li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:утроба.html>утро́ба</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">utroba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ǫtroba</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">internal organs</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утроба.html>утро́ба</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">utróba</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утроба.html>утро́бы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утроба.html>утро́бы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утроба.html>утро́б</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>womb</li>
<li>belly</li></ol>

***утруждать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:утруждать.html>утружда́ть</a> (17967)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">утруди́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">utrudítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утруждать.html>утружда́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">utruždátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">утруди́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to trouble, to bother
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хо́чет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:утруждать.html>утружда́ть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on ne xóčet sebjá <b>utruždátʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he doesn't want to take the trouble [to be bothered]</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***утыкать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:утыкать.html>утыка́ть</a> (20989)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тыкать.html>ты́кать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">týkatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утыкать.html>утыка́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">utykátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уткнуть.html>уткну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bury, to hide
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:утыкать.html>утыка́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воротник.html>воротни́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>utykatʹ</b> licó v vorotník</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bury one's face in one's collar</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:утыкать.html>утыка́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нос.html>нос</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>utykatʹ</b> nos v knígu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bury oneself in a book</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тыкать.html>ты́кать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">týkatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:утыкаться.html>утыка́ться</a> (28812)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утыкать.html>утыка́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">utykátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утыкаться.html>утыка́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">utykátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уткнуться.html>уткну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bury oneself <i>(in)</i>, to hide <i>(one's face)</i> <i>(in)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:утыкаться.html>утыка́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:угол.html>у́гол</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>utykátʹsja</b> v úgol</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hide (one's face) in a corner</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:утыкаться.html>утыка́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голово́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подушка.html>поду́шку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>utykátʹsja</b> golovój v podúšku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bury one's head in the pillow</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:утыкаться.html>утыка́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нос.html>но́сом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>utykátʹsja</b> nósom v knígu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bury oneself in a book</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come to rest <i>(upon, against)</i>, to be stopped <i>(by)</i>, to hit</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:утыкать.html>утыка́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">utykátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:утюг.html>утю́г</a> (7721)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> source, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Turkic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Turkic language">Old Turkic</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small> <i>ütüg</i>; whence also Turkish <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">ütü</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">iron</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
